Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Points

Strengthening the People's Foundation 193

— Chen

Mr. Wang Yiting, a leader in Shanghai's business community, recently told a reporter from the New Voice Society that the current state of economic decline in our country is extremely precarious. The foundation of a country lies in its people, and if the people's foundation is shaken, how can the country stand? Based on his qualifications as a merchant, he observed the lack of silver reserves in the country and the increasingly sophisticated methods of foreign powers manipulating finance. He believed that our country's situation was difficult and in urgent need of reform. Therefore, he submitted a proposal to the authorities, urging them to establish concrete measures as soon as possible to cope with the situation and strengthen the people's foundation.

Our country has always had a famous saying: "The country is established by the people, and the people exist with the country." If this sentence is interpreted in a "modern" way, it means that the existence of the country lies in protecting and enriching the people, and the happiness of the people lies in having a strong and independent country. In fact, these two are two aspects of the same thing. The strength of the country lies in whether there are prosperous people, and the prosperity of the people can determine the strength of the country; otherwise, this country contains internal contradictions.

Because in our country's situation, recently, the industrial decline, the rural bankruptcy, and it's increasingly developing into a financial crisis and a fiscal crisis. Especially after the implementation of the American silver policy, the outflow of Chinese silver has extremely shaken China's currency unit. The great powers at this time are expressing various "good intentions" of "helping" China, advocating that China should establish connections with the US dollar, British pound, gold, etc. Of course, if we still want to strengthen the people's foundation firmly, these kindnesses are difficult for us to accept.

However, if China's currency value is to be stable and avoid financial and fiscal crises, we must first balance international payments. To balance international payments, we must curb the large-scale import of foreign goods and revive our country's industry and agriculture. Therefore, we advise those who are working hard to "strengthen the people's foundation" to ask themselves how to create the preconditions for achieving this goal. Otherwise, the "people's foundation" will have no way to be strengthened, and the founding of the country will become a major problem.

A Walk in the Deep Mountains on a Summer Night 194

— Xin Er

Mountains, shady forests, ancient temples, pavilions, the sound of bells, white houses, young people, soft and low murmurs, all shrouded in the misty, bright, silvery gauze, silver mist-like moonlight, an endless expanse of haziness, drunk and wanting to dissolve; people, as if in a dream, on the moon in the sky: the hearts of young people, so fluttering?

"Float! Float to the ends of the earth... Float to..."

Slowly turning their gaze to the mountaintop, trembling with joy

"Look, that moon rising upwards, that golden plate, that..."

Like a golden fruit that can be plucked with a hand, forgetting that this is the human world. The surroundings are quiet, solemn, and beautifully tranquil. The light and refreshing breeze of Lingnan, incessantly blowing through the gray-white pavilion open on all sides, several young people in the pavilion, collapsed on the terrazzo floor, leaning against the pillars, not lost in thought, but immersed in a realm beyond the mundane, suddenly, someone slowly, gently said:

"Let's go, take advantage of the moonlight to walk at night!"

"Oh,... the cool breeze is so wonderful, the night is so intoxicating, slowly..." A companion responded slowly, as if reciting poetry.

Page 18

On hot summer nights, this Han Mountain Valley by the Han River, more cool and beautiful than the seaside, the foothills, have all become good places to escape the summer heat, a dreamland for young people. At night, they often abandon their stuffy dormitories, go to the cool pavilions on the mountain foothills to cool off, sometimes falling asleep leisurely, reluctant to return even in the middle of the night. The school vacation has begun, and the people inside the white houses are all restless. Mothers urge them to return, and homesickness stirs, so they pack their luggage with their fellow villagers and return home. The route back home is full of towering mountains and ridges, young people, in order to accustom their feet to the stinging thorns on the path of life, do not sit in sedan chairs carried by others, willingly letting their tender feet be pricked and worn by the thorns. But in the fierce summer sun, the stifling heat is like being burned while climbing endless high mountains and sloping ridges, which is often daunting for young people. So they pat each other on the chest and shout—don't be afraid! It's good to walk in the cool of the night!

Take an umbrella, wear thin short shirts and trousers, carry a small bag, and cheerfully and heroically go to the cool pavilion, waiting for the moon to rise before setting off. However, the night is cool and the moonlight is beautiful, the beauty of the mountains intoxicates and keeps people lingering, slowly and slowly, delaying the departure.

"Don't fall asleep! The cool night is intoxicating, but the journey must be taken!"

The moon rises higher, the night becomes more beautiful, the travelers become more intoxicated, leisurely, densely, but the time of deep intoxication passes especially quickly. The croaking of frogs gradually intensifies:

"Friends, let's go! It's almost midnight, let's go! That distant and difficult journey!"

Several times urging each other, several times struggling, dragging soft and deeply intoxicated legs forward: go! Go!, the heroic and beautiful voices of young people, resound in the beautiful and intoxicated night.

Looking ahead, the night curtain hangs deeply, a piece of haziness: in the distance, lush and verdant, mountains and sky, blocking the way. Distant, boundless, the tender hearts of young people, will tremble slightly. However, we must go! The road that must be taken! Lift up your spirits, embolden yourself, and hurry on your way firmly. Breaking through the dark mountain valleys, the shadowy winding paths, the grass nests, and then turning into even darker mountain hollows, one stage after another, deathly silent, quiet, desolate to the point of extinction, desolate, only the misty and faint moonlight, leaking out from the cloud crevices, stealing a photo, allowing pedestrians to walk, in addition, the wind gently shakes the mountains and forests, playing a sad and low whispering rustling sound, human shadows, footsteps, lonely travelers, constantly emboldening themselves, step by step climbing up, the soles of their feet drunk and sore, people tired, but, the journey is long, so we can only keep walking: ahead is the endless dark deep mountain.

In this deep mountain night, the young people, again discover that there are fellow travelers between the mountain hollows ahead. Unconsciously, they gather more courage, echoing each other with loud shouts, hurrying to catch up:

Panting as they catch up, the tired hearts of the young people are even more ashamed. It turns out to be a team of male and female coolies, carrying loads of about a hundred pounds on their injured shoulders, gasping and panting as they move forward, their tense expressions, their voices, make people feel tragic! Their lives are even harder! They not only have to walk this thorny mountain road in the dark night, but also have to bear this heavy burden on their shoulders, and yet they still struggle hard, young and unburdened people, how should they work doubly hard! The hearts of the travelers, are moved by the hard-working coolies. They continue to walk in a large group: "Go! Friends, take advantage of the dark night to hurry on the road, finish the dark night, and wait for dawn to reach your destination;"

The Cultural Street of Beiping 195

— Yueshan

Some people call Beiping a "cultural city," but in fact, the material foundation of modern culture in Beiping seems to be less solid than that of Shanghai. Take a few of the more famous bookstores, for example: the Commercial Press, the Zhonghua Book Company, and their main factories are all in Shanghai; and so on, the Guanming Book Company, the Modern Book Company, and other bookstores, only have branches in Beiping. In terms of distribution and printing, all the bookstores seem to think that Shanghai is more convenient than Beiping, and in reality, Shanghai is indeed more convenient than Beiping; then the name "cultural city" seems to should be given to Shanghai, so why is Beiping the cultural city instead?

Thinking carefully, Beiping is neither a commercial city, nor a political city, nor an industrial city, and in terms of population, it is the second largest city in the country; it seems inappropriate not to give such a large city sitting in the second position a more beautiful name. So, comparatively speaking, Beiping is still a cultural city; anyway, Beiping has enough professors and students, and enough poets and men of letters, so it is not too much, or too untrue to call it a cultural city. I think, this is the origin of the "cultural city."

Let's take a look at the cultural street in the cultural city.

Don't misunderstand, thinking that there is really a street in Beiping called Cultural Street; there isn't. Cultural Street is Liulichang, commonly known as Changdian. Liulichang doesn't actually have any factories that actually make glass, it's just called that; this is like Songshu Street not necessarily having pine trees, Yangrou Hutong not necessarily having mutton, and so on; it's just called that. As for why, even the oldest of the old Beiping people can't figure it out, let alone me.

As for why Liulichang is called Cultural Street, I do know this. The reason is: there are many bookstores, many stationery shops, many shops selling paintings and calligraphy, and many shops selling antiques and curios. Let me say something interesting: the signs of the "cultural shops" (let's call them that) in Cultural Street are all written quite impressively, there are absolutely no ugly ones, or bad ones, from this point alone, you can see a bit of the flavor of Cultural Street.

To put it more practically, Cultural Street should not only be Liulichang, Yangmeizhu Slanting Street outside the east entrance of Liulichang should also be called Cultural Street, the World Book Company, the Kaiming Bookstore, and other bookstores are on that Slanting Street, and there are also quite a few antique and stationery shops; but compared to Liulichang, it always seems to be inferior. Cultural Street and Slanting Street both run east-west, separated by a street with an interesting name: Yichi Dajie (One-Foot Street), Yichi Dajie is not long or big, it is just slightly curved, separating Cultural Street and Slanting Street; otherwise, Slanting Street could very well be named Liulichang and share the name of Cultural Street.

No matter what, the area from Liulichang to Yangmeizhu Slanting Street always has some cultural color. Most of the "cultural shops" in this area still sell old books, followed by calligraphy and painting shops (mounting and rubbing shops belong to this category), the fewest are the few shops selling new books. From this, you can also see the general picture of Cultural Street. Beiping is, after all, a place where men of letters have frequented for many years, so there are naturally more things like old books and old calligraphy. The first half of the first month of the solar and lunar years is the period when Changdian is open. The so-called opening is just adding a temporary market to join in the fun. During the opening period, from Hepingmen through Normal University to the southern end of Nan Xinhua Street, there is a street two li long, full of stalls selling old books and old calligraphy, and men of letters naturally frequent it; this shows the power of old books in Beiping.

In the new book industry, only the facade of the Commercial Press is beautiful, with a building; this is the only building in Cultural Street, and I imagine it must be different from the cultural street in Shanghai with its rows of tall buildings. Cultural Street is just like the cultural city, old and simple; old books and old calligraphy support Cultural Street, and the power of new books is not great in Cultural Street. As for new magazines and other books, the sales locations are no longer Cultural Street, Dong'an Market and Xidan Market are their strongholds, and buying magazines and going to Cultural Street will mostly be disappointed.

Lotus 196

— Hu Sizhong

I haven't seen lotus flowers for a long time. This time, when I came home, I saw a pot of lotus flowers in the courtyard, just budding and waiting to bloom, and I was extremely happy in my heart. The ancients said, "The lotus is the gentleman among flowers." This statement is not the reason why I love camellias, because I am not a so-called upper-class gentleman. According to the principle of gathering things by category and having personal preferences, I naturally would not use the qualifications of a gentleman to appreciate and compare plants that are like gentlemen. I love it, but I'd rather say it's the prompting of the environment and based on the inherent nature of loving nature. For several years, I've been trapped in the city of Shanghai, with streets full of smoke and dust, and dense clusters of houses like beehives. It's really quite difficult to see a little bit of light and simple plants. Moreover, being suppressed by life, I don't have time to go to Chinese-style gardens like Bansong Garden to admire some verdant plants. Recently, I was fortunate to have an opportunity to escape to the quiet countryside, and seeing the elegant plants in my own home refreshed my spirit and vision, how could it not make people happy?

In addition, the lotus flower is indeed a plant worthy of love. Look at those round leaves, with a verdant and elegant color, supported on graceful and gentle branches, swaying in the wind, truly lovely. Even those small tender leaves, draped on the water surface, or curled up tender leaves, using small and delicate tender branches, supporting like a small umbrella, shading under the large leaves, are as cute as petite and delicate infants. The flower buds grow from a small bud, all the way until they are budding and waiting to bloom, they have already grown to be like radiant young girls. When the flower hearts bloom in full bloom, and the green petals turn white, revealing individual white stamens in a pot of green, it is truly pleasing to see. If the flower heart is further unfolded, and the yellow stamens are inverted like hanging tassels, attracting one or two small bees to soar there, that would be even more interesting.

When I came home, I encountered many rainy days. I didn't go out for a long day, so I quietly sat in front of the courtyard, appreciating that pot of elegant color. In the rain, the lotus flower is even more lovely. The leaves, being struck by raindrops, tilt slightly, and the raindrops slip on the smooth leaf surface, and then slip out, dripping and shattering on the ground, like the smashing of pearls. Sometimes the concave part of the leaf heart is filled with raindrops, unable to pour out, so they roll roundly and continuously on the leaf heart, which is even more beautiful. The lotus flower in the rain is even more lovely, the petals are wetted by rainwater, and they feel fresher, giving people a kind of fresh taste. The rain threads stir up wrinkles on the water surface, and on a pot of mud, the water surface is exceptionally clear, which is truly helpful in clearing the mood.

For the lotus, it can also evoke a little bit of warm memories, which was in the year I was seventeen. At that time, the school was on summer vacation, and I was living in the countryside. Every evening, I always walked with my classmate, Miss Lin, together by a lotus pond. In the moment when the evening breeze swept through, smelling the bursts of fragrance carried by the wind, watching the swimming fish swim in the gaps between the lotus stems, and because of the vastness of the pond and the countless lotus flowers, so that the eyes were full of pure white stamens, stirring up pure emotions in the hearts of the two people, we often walked until late at night before going back to sleep. If it was a moonlit night, we would be even more delighted. At that time, the tea leaves were lush, and the dewdrops on the leaf surface, reflecting the moonlight, were crystal clear and very lovely. In the quiet countryside, with eyes full of fields, a pool of shallow water, and the fragrance wafting in the air, it is deeply evocative to imagine the pure and simple mood of the young people, and the warm words that were inspired by it. Later, as I rushed around, the pure friendship was lost, and I rarely saw the beautiful lotus flowers. Now, I can only see this small pot in my own courtyard in my hometown, which is also a consolation. And the lost warm memories make people love friendship and lotus flowers together, which can be said to be the reason why I love lotus flowers.

Red Eggs 197

— Jing Jia

My wife's belly is getting bigger day by day, and when friends meet, they always shout:

"Congratulations, congratulations! When are you treating us to red eggs?"

On the surface, I always deal with them with a smile, but in my heart, their congratulatory voices are simply like a steel knife specially stabbing my heart!

I am not a person who dislikes children, and I always have a happy heart when I see the children of relatives, friends, and neighbors. No matter how troubled I am, as long as I see a child, I will feel relieved. Since getting married, I have been hoping to have a child as soon as possible, but now that this hope is about to be realized, my heart feels like it has a big stone on it. A kind of unbearable worry has been growing in my heart as my wife's belly gets bigger!

A child is indeed an angel in a family, and he can offer a lot of happiness to the family. However, there must be considerable conditions to have such an angel. Without considerable conditions, even if there is a child, it is just a burden. Like me, I am definitely not qualified to be the father of a little angel. My monthly income is only enough to maintain the minimum living standard of the two of us, and it will be difficult to live if we add another person. In this situation, how can I deserve a little angel! It's just a burden!

My wife also loves children, and when she found out she was pregnant, she was so happy that she cried with laughter. She was always fantasizing about everything after having a child. She said that she would be a good mother and turn the child into a strong man. From a young age, she would give him good habits, keep him clean, not be greedy, not make trouble, not waste, not... In the future, she would send him to school so that he would be knowledgeable and be able to contribute to the country, and also bring honor to his parents...

In order not to break my wife's sweet dreams, I always smiled and agreed with her opinions. She said, "I want to buy a sailor suit for the child," I agreed; she said she wanted to buy high-end toys for the child, I agreed; she said, "In the future, I want to send the child to better schools, even if the tuition is more expensive, it doesn't matter," I also agreed. I would rather break my own heart, but I don't want to destroy her fantasies of happiness.

However, my wife's sweet dream was ultimately broken by herself. She noticed that I often frowned, and earnestly asked me if I had any hidden pain. At first, I deceived her with irrelevant words, but later I couldn't hide it. I had to sigh and say:

"I also want to turn the child into a promising person, but, many farmers' children have extraordinary talents, but they didn't become great people, but just remained farmers, there's nothing poor people can do! Let's not talk about the future, even when the child is born, and friends ask us for red eggs, it will be unbearable enough!"

So, an extremely unbearable hidden pain also grew in my wife's heart. She no longer fantasized, and she also felt that a child was not something that our kind of family should have.

Now, my wife is about to give birth. Every time friends ask us for red eggs, we don't even have the courage to put on a smiling mask and deal with them.

Red eggs can only be had under considerable conditions!

The sound film "Two Brothers" will soon be seen by audiences.

The new film "Welcoming Spring Song" will be directed by Gao Lihen.

Shao Renrou, the assistant manager of Tianyi, arrived in Shanghai yesterday from Hong Kong.

"Grace of a Beauty" will soon be shown in various ports.

Opening of Cangzhou Garden Cinema 202

The Cangzhou Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road, now, for the sake of providing coolness and entertainment for all sectors, spared no expense to open the never-before-opened Cangzhou Garden as an open-air cinema, equipped with Western Electric Company's sound equipment. Shepherd Boy Hero and Beauty 203

In the Yi Hua Film Company, the "shepherd boy," "hero," and "beauty" were discovered.

The shepherd boy is Ying Yunwei, the director of "Hero of the Times." It turned out that one day, while filming under the scorching sun, Ying Yunwei fashioned an extraordinarily large straw hat in the props room and put it on his head, resembling a shepherd boy on the back of a cow. However, Qiu Yiwei pointed to Zhang Jiaxiang in "Iron Rooster," because Zhang Jiaxiang's words led to Ying Wei, who is Shang Guanwu. Goodness, this gentleman is so tall that one would immediately imagine the demeanor of Xiang Yu, the Conqueror of Chu. Jiang Xiu said that Shang Guanwu had co-starred with Xu Qin芳in "Farewell My Concubine" and "went wild," almost scaring away the spirit of Yu Ji. It can be seen that he looks like a hero. Ying Yunwei invited him to play the hero in "Hero of the Times," which is truly what the people of Shanghai call "matching his appetite."

But where is the beauty? Don't rush: Look, as the gauze window is moved, the musk fragrance assaults the senses, and a figure is faintly revealed, with stunning beauty. Who is this person? She is the hero's object, the beauty Hu Ping! Hu Ping plays the beauty in "Hero of the Times," and her magic is great. It is often said that when her delicate eyebrows are slightly raised, the hero becomes anxious. Ying Yunwei's technique shows considerable skill. When it is screened in the future, it will surely move people's hearts to the utmost.

Eight Major Stars Co-star in "Black Shadow," to be Screened at the Jin Cheng Grand Theatre 204

The domestically produced detective masterpiece "Black Shadow," a great production by the Great Wall Film Company, will soon be screened at the Jin Cheng Grand Theatre. The film stars Gao Zhanfei, Wang Yuanlong, Hu Ping, Zhang Meiyu, Shang Guanwu, Yuan Congmei, Zhang Zhizhi, and Xu Huayuan. In addition, Chen Dabei and Wu Wenchao also play important roles in the film. The story tells of a cunning and vicious young man who is blinded by greed and commits a series of bloody crimes. Moreover, the methods he uses to kill are elusive and unpredictable, leaving the great detective helpless. The plot is full of twists and turns, captivating the audience and immersing them in an atmosphere of terror and confusion from beginning to end. Recently, movie fans seem to be extremely interested in detective films, such as "Covering One's Body in Courage," which recently premiered at the Da Guangming Theatre, has achieved great success in terms of box office revenue. Therefore, it is expected that the premiere of "Black Shadow" will cause a sensation, not only because it is a detective film, but also because so many stars are co-starring in a film, which is a miracle that has never happened before in the domestic film industry.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Automobile Weekly

Overview of the 1935 Buick New Car 207

— Yun

Since 1935, the Buick Motor Company has joined the low-price car industry, providing another new contribution to the automotive industry. This contribution is none other than the company's newly released six-cylinder car. This product is comparable to the company's improved and perfected straight-eight-cylinder car. All the important reforms and progress that the company implemented on the eight-cylinder car last year, as well as all the design and construction features, are also available on this lower-priced six-cylinder car. The six-cylinder car's body styles include two-door and four-door sedans, two-door convertible sedans, coupe, sports coupe, and multi-purpose coupe, among others.

One of the most prominent features of the 1935 Buick car is that its engineers were uniquely able to achieve the ultimate streamlined design and implement it on the entire car, while at the same time ensuring that it was just right, without being bizarre, which would detract from the aesthetic appeal. This is a unique feature of Buick and is already widely appreciated, so there is no need to elaborate. However, when considering the success of this novel style, the credit should first be given to the adoption of the Fisher No Draft Ventilation Solid Steel "Turret Top" body. The safety, comfort, and aesthetics of this structure have reached their peak and are incomparable to any previous Fisher body. The entire solid steel roof is supported on steel brackets and welded together with the other steel parts of the body, making it extremely strong. Thus, passengers in the car are surrounded by steel armor, making their absolute safety self-evident.

Another feature of the new Buick car that differs from previous structures is the use of greatly improved hydraulic brakes, equipped with double-layer and triple-layer sealed brake drums, which are not vulnerable to water and dust. The new car doors are much wider, especially on the two-door models, making it easier to get in and out and more comfortable. All models have more interior space, and the seats are wider. Headroom has been greatly increased. As for the split front seats of the two-door models, they are a new creation and particularly outstanding. The radiator and engine cover are beautiful and pleasing to the eye. The wing panels and headlights are streamlined. The V-shaped windshield has always been a feature of the car body, and Buick is the first to use it on low-priced cars.

The luggage compartment space on all new Buick cars has generally increased. Sedan models have a special luggage compartment in the rear, where the spare tire can also be stored. As for convertible sedan models, the luggage space is even more spacious due to the installation of a luggage rack. In terms of mechanics, the various improvements of the new Buick car are too numerous to mention. The knee-action part is now mounted on a 2 3/4-inch torque tube, making it more robust and comfortable. As for the steering ratio, it has now been increased to 17.5:1, making steering easier. The entire electrical system has greatly increased in capacity, making starting easier. As for the various improvements in the carburetor manifold, the warm-up time required for starting is shortened. In addition, the lubrication and cooling systems remain the same. In terms of mechanics, the most noteworthy feature is the silver alloy connecting rod bearing, which is much more resistant to the high temperatures generated during high-speed driving than any metal used before. The new Buick car is even stronger than the 1934 model. In terms of weight, the six-cylinder four-door car weighs 3,400 pounds, while the extended eight-cylinder car weighs 3,550 pounds. In short, Buick has improved and perfected every aspect of the engine, chassis, and body, making it impeccable. This is why its safety, reliability, comfort, utility, and economy are all outstanding.

Shanghai Public Concession Summer Car Registration Statistics 208

— Yu

The summer car registration statistics for the Shanghai Public Concession in 1935 have recently been released by the Public Works Department. These statistics cover the period up to the end of June this year. The total number of cars, including passenger cars, trucks, and public buses, is 9,584. Of these, 7,426 are passenger cars, 1,994 are trucks, and 164 are public buses. Passenger cars are further divided into public and private categories. There are 501 public cars and 6,925 private cars. Among the trucks, 1,203 are privately owned and 791 are publicly owned. In addition, the number of registered motorcycles is 750. All of the above statistics do not include cars and vehicles used by the military forces of various countries stationed in Shanghai.

A total of 154 different car brands are registered. Ford accounts for the largest number, with a total of 1,135 cars. Austin is second with 633 cars, followed by Chevrolet with 590 cars. The breakdown of private and public cars is as follows: (1) Ford: 1,032 private cars and 103 public cars, totaling 1,135 cars. (2) Austin: 633 private cars. (3) Chevrolet: 369 private cars and 221 public cars, totaling 590 cars. (4) Buick: 567 private cars and 6 public cars, totaling 573 cars. (5) Fisher: 368 private cars. (6) Morris Cowley: 318 private cars. (7) Studebaker: 289 private cars and 7 public cars, totaling 296 cars. (8) Dodge: 229 private cars and 37 public cars, totaling 266 cars. (9) Plymouth: 228 private cars and 16 public cars, totaling 244 cars. (10) Nash: 215 private cars and 11 public cars, totaling 226 cars.

In addition to the above, more noteworthy brands include Auburn with 39 private cars; Chrysler with 160 private cars and 2 public cars, totaling 162 cars; Citroen with 108 private cars; Continental Beacon with 20 private cars and 4 public cars, totaling 24 cars; DeSoto with 47 private cars and 2 public cars, totaling 49 cars; Durant with 21 private cars and 1 public car, totaling 22 cars; Erskine with 53 private cars; Essex Terraplane with 173 private cars; Graham-Paige with 41 private cars and 4 public cars, totaling 45 cars; Hillman with 46 private cars (including Baby); Hudson with 67 private cars; Hupmobile with 83 private cars and 2 public cars, totaling 85 cars; Lincoln with 6 private cars; Morris Minor with 24 private cars; Morris 8 with 180 private cars; Morris Oxford with 156 private cars; Morris 12 with 3 private cars. The above are all private cars. Willys-Overland with 23 private cars; Willys-Knight with 62 private cars; Auburn with 67 private cars; Willys with 8 private cars. The following are all private cars. Willys-Knight with 119 private cars and 79 public cars, totaling 198 cars; Packard with 55 private cars; Pierce-Arrow with 9 private cars; Pontiac with 90 private cars and 5 public cars; Renault with 69 private cars; Rogan with 54 private cars; Rolls-Royce with 10 private cars; Star with 39 private cars; Standard with 127 private cars; Terraplane with 60 private cars; Vauxhall with 67 private cars; Whippet with 20 private cars; Willys-Knight with 36 private cars. The following are all private cars. The registration of trucks also has Ford the most, recording (1) Ford with 390 private trucks and 100 public trucks, for a total of 490. (2) Chevrolet at 108 + 54 totaling 162 trucks. (3) Stewart 42 + 108 for a total of 150 trucks. (4) Tilling-Stevens 139 all as passenger public buses. (5) Fageol at 47 + 82 for a total of 129 trucks. (6) Studebaker at 39 + 86 for a total of 125 trucks. (7) G.M.C. 41 + 58 for a total of 99 trucks. (8) Reo 33 + 63 totaling 96 trucks. (9) Morris at 77 + 9 for a total of 86 trucks.
